FTP Manager Pro automatically retries to establish the connection.\r\n\r\nBackup your connection profiles\r\nWant to move FTP Manager Pro on another computer without recreating all the profiles? This enhances the security and control over file transfers in and outside of the network.\r\n\r\nTrial\r\nFTP Manager Pro provides a free 7-day trial.
